msg:Staying in Hilton for a long time, the overall feeling is that the appearance is basically high-end, and the room is so-so. This one is the opposite. The appearance is ordinary, the lobby is small, but the room is very good. There are only 3 Hiltons in Zhejiang. I have stayed in Zhuji and this one. Let's compare them. Zhuji's appearance is very cool, the sky lobby is full of style, and the room and bedding are not too bad. This one is the opposite. Summarize the following points for your reference:
1. Cost-effectiveness and service: The price of this Hilton is really super cheap. I booked the cheapest comfortable king-size bed room for a casual one-night stay. The front desk directly upgraded me to a landscape room on the executive floor (46th floor) for free. There are floor-to-ceiling windows on both sides. I was touched.
2. Bedding: Serta's mattress is moderately soft and hard, with a pair of goose down hard pillows and soft pillows. The four-piece set is better, but it is still insufficient compared with the Marriott series. I certainly can't compare with Westin, so I won't say it. Many of Marriott's use Simmons and a down comfort pad. My family uses King Koil, and I stay in Slumberland more often. To be honest, it is more comfortable than Hilton. In addition, Marriott's pillows are all incense, which Hilton can't compare with.
3. Room type: Very good, this is the invincible place, separate cloakroom, washroom, bathtub and entrance, a small room is divided into many small rooms, very good.
4. Bathtub: The bathtub is average, Marriott InterContinental usually gives bath salts.
5. Breakfast: Very rich.
Summary: Hilton's appearance is invincible among all hotels, but other aspects can only be said to be relatively balanced, without any special highlights.

msg:The hotel is still very good, the attitude of the service staff is very friendly, and you can feel a lot of careful thoughts in the details. Five-star praise.
I drove to the hotel with my family at around 2:30 pm. There may be some problems in the connection between the hotel and Ctrip system. Although I booked two rooms in one order, the front desk seemed to only recognize that I booked one room when checking in with my name. The other room was handled after providing the information of the other person, which is different from the usual check-in experience.
One room is on the 38th floor and the other is on the 30th floor, which is far apart. Fortunately, the room numbers are the same on different floors. They are all along the corridor to the innermost room at the end. The room is very bright, and the warm afternoon sunlight can supplement a lot of calcium.
If you look closely, you can find some mottled traces on the air-conditioning vents of the room on the 38th floor, which makes people feel the accumulation of years in this old hotel.
Later, after communicating with the front desk, I changed to another room type on the 38th floor. The room is much larger. I like the efficiency of the front desk in handling problems in a timely manner!
Later, because there was no small spoon in the room, I asked the front desk and it was delivered quickly. In addition, the hand soap that is usually available in the hotel has become hand sanitizer. I originally wanted a piece, but I have already bothered the front desk several times, so I was too embarrassed to give up.
In general, for a weekend in Jiaxing of about 700 yuan, it is probably worth the price. It is recommended that friends who stay in this hotel upgrade their rooms to avoid a lot of troublesome communication. After all, the most important thing when traveling is to have fun.
